\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_class}{Class}} representing a list of output generators that are written to in parallel.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{writeCodeLink()}{writeCodeLink()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Output\+List\+::write\+Code\+Link (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2src_2types_8h_a55cbcb91fc25e3a2e785b8a30309843c}{Code\+Symbol\+Type}}}]{type,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} \&}]{ref,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} \&}]{file,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} \&}]{anchor,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} \&}]{name,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} \&}]{tooltip }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Writes a link to an object in a code fragment. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em type} & The type of symbol, used for semantic syntax highlighting, may be Default is no info is available. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & If this is non-\/zero, the object is to be found in an external documentation file. \\
\hline
{\em file} & The file in which the object is located. \\
\hline
{\em anchor} & The anchor uniquely identifying the object within the file. \\
\hline
{\em name} & The text to display as a placeholder for the link. \\
\hline
{\em tooltip} & The tooltip to display when the mouse is on the link. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}


Implements \mbox{\hyperlink{class_code_output_interface_a13a6b8760052adea7080330705d4a020}{Code\+Output\+Interface}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Output\+List\+::write\+Object\+Link (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} \&}]{ref,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} \&}]{file,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} \&}]{anchor,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} \&}]{name }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Writes a link to an object in the documentation. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ref} & If this is non-\/zero, the object is to be found in an external documentation file. \\
\hline
{\em file} & The file in which the object is located. \\
\hline
{\em anchor} & The anchor uniquely identifying the object within the file. \\
\hline
{\em name} & The text to display as a placeholder for the link. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
